[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing campaign on the `exif_from_data_fuzzer` target uncovered a [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in the libexif library. AddressSanitizer reports a one-byte [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread past the end of a dynamically allocated buffer while parsing FUJI maker‐note [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata. The out-of-bounds access originates in the utility function `exif_get_slong` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mand its sibling `exif_get_long`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is invoked during the FUJI maker‐note load[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutine.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash is classified as a heap-buffer-overflow: the code attempts to read one [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte beyond an allocated [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte memory region.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Crash context  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness calls `exif_data_new_from_data`, which in turn invokes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. During EXIF parsing, `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load` is called to interpret FUJI [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker‐note tags.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Inside that routine, `exif_get_long` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand its signed variant `exif_get_slong`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads multi-byte values from the provided buffer without sufficient bounds checks. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. AddressSanitizer pinpoints the invalid read at offset [0m[1;36m0x11f[0m[39m, seven bytes past [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of the [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte allocation.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The vulnerable code paths are in `libexif/exif-utils.[0m[1;92mc:137[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_get_slong`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `libexif/exif-utils.[0m[1;92mc:167[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_get_long`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow surfaces only when parsing FUJI-specific metadata in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:175[0m[39m`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The issue is reproducible under libFuzzer with minimal seed corpus and appears [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon any input that triggers the FUJI maker-note parser with insufficient data.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Bounds checking logic in `exif_get_slong` and `exif_get_long` [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlibexif/exif-utils.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The FUJI maker-note loader in `exif-mnote-data-fuji.c`, especially how buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlengths and offsets are validated prior to field extraction.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. General EXIF data loading in `exif-data.c` to understand how input buffers are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed down and whether higher-level checks exist.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis overflow vulnerability suggests missing or inadequate range checks when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading integers from untrusted EXIF data. A thorough review of buffer management [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the EXIF parsing pipeline—particularly around maker-note sections—is warranted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto assess the full impact and identify similar issues.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma small buffer when computing a maker-note pointer without sufficient bounds [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks. The patch attempt inserts explicit `CHECKOVERFLOW` guards before the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte reads, logs an error, and returns early on underflow. However, applying [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A libFuzzer run against `exif_from_data_fuzzer` triggers an AddressSanitizer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror:  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  *“heap-buffer-overflow on address … READ of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m”*  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The stack trace shows the overflow happens in exif_get_slong [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif-utils.[0m[1;92mc:137[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalled via exif_get_long in the Fuji maker-note loader [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_mnote_data_fuji_load`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer in question is allocated based on the input size supplied to the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer. In `exif_mnote_data_fuji_load`, code computes `datao = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately does `[0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without verifying that `datao [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` lies within `buf_size`. This leads to out-of-bounds reads when `datao` is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtoo large.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
